-- Secventa DDL pentru crearea tabelei TITLE_DETAIL
---------------------------------------------------

prompt 
prompt 1. Crearea tabelei TITLE_DETAIL
prompt ===============================

CREATE TABLE TITLE_DETAIL
(
   TITLE_ID NUMBER(4),
   COD_CAEN NUMBER(11),
   TITLE_DETAIL NVARCHAR2(150)
) ;

-- Secventa DDL pentru crearea tabelei TITLES
---------------------------------------------------

prompt 
prompt 2. Crearea tabelei TITLES
prompt ======================
 
CREATE TABLE TITLES
(
   EMP_NO NUMBER(4),
   TITLE_ID NUMBER(4) 
) ;

-- Secventa DDL pentru crearea tabelei DEPARTMENTS
---------------------------------------------------

prompt
prompt 3. Crearea tabelei DEPARTMENTS
prompt ==============================

CREATE TABLE DEPARTMENTS
(
   DEPT_NO CHAR(2),
   DEPT_NAME VARCHAR2(40)
) ;
---------------------------------------------------
-- Secventa DDL pentru crearea tabelei DEPT_EMP
---------------------------------------------------

prompt
prompt 4. Crearea tabelei DEPT_EMP
prompt ===========================

CREATE TABLE DEPT_EMP
(
   EMP_NO NUMBER(4),
   DEPT_NO CHAR(2),
   FROM_DATE DATE,
   TO_DATE DATE
) ;
---------------------------------------------------
-- Secventa DDL pentru crearea tabelei DEPT_MANAGER
---------------------------------------------------

prompt
prompt 5. Crearea tabelei DEPT_MANAGER
prompt ===============================

CREATE TABLE DEPT_MANAGER
(
   DEPT_NO CHAR(2),  
   EMP_NO NUMBER(4),
   FROM_DATE DATE,
   TO_DATE DATE
) ;
---------------------------------------------------
-- Secventa DDL pentru crearea tabelei EMPLOYEE
---------------------------------------------------

prompt 
prompt 6. Crearea tabelei EMPLOYEES
prompt ============================

CREATE TABLE EMPLOYEES
(
   EMP_NO NUMBER(4),
   BIRTH_DATE DATE,
   FIRST_NAME VARCHAR2(14),
   LAST_NAME VARCHAR2(16),
   GENDER CHAR(1) CHECK (GENDER IN ('M','F')),
   HIRE_DATE DATE
) ;

---------------------------------------------------
-- Secventa DDL pentru crearea tabelei SALARIES
---------------------------------------------------

prompt
prompt 7. Crearea tabelei SALARIES
prompt ===========================

CREATE TABLE SALARIES
(
   EMP_NO NUMBER(4),
   PIC_ID NUMBER(4),
   SALARY NUMBER(6),
   FROM_DATE DATE,
   TO_DATE DATE
) ;

CREATE TABLE PICTURES
(
    PIC_ID NUMBER(4),
    PICTURE BLOB
);

prompt Au fost incarcate 80 inregistrari in tabela SALARIES...
prompt =======================================================

----------------------------------------------------------------
-- Restrictii de tip cheie primara pentru tabela TITLE_DETAIL
----------------------------------------------------------------
ALTER TABLE TITLE_DETAIL ADD CONSTRAINT TITLE_ID_PK PRIMARY KEY(TITLE_ID) ENABLE;
----------------------------------------------------------------
-- Restrictii de tip cheie primara pentru tabela DEPARTMENTS
----------------------------------------------------------------
ALTER TABLE DEPARTMENTS ADD CONSTRAINT DEPT_NO_PK PRIMARY KEY(DEPT_NO) ENABLE;
----------------------------------------------------------------
-- Restrictii de tip cheie primara pentru tabela EMPLOYEES
----------------------------------------------------------------
ALTER TABLE EMPLOYEES ADD CONSTRAINT EMP_NO_PK PRIMARY KEY(EMP_NO) ENABLE;
----------------------------------------------------------------
-- Restrictii de tip cheie straina pentru tabela TITLES
----------------------------------------------------------------
ALTER TABLE TITLES ADD CONSTRAINT TIT_DET_TIT_TITLE_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY(TITLE_ID)
        REFERENCES TITLE_DETAIL(TITLE_ID) ENABLE;
ALTER TABLE TITLES ADD CONSTRAINT EMP_TIT_EMP_NO_FK FOREIGN KEY(EMP_NO)
        REFERENCES EMPLOYEES(EMP_NO) ENABLE;
----------------------------------------------------------------
-- Restrictii de tip cheie straina pentru tabela DEPT_EMP
----------------------------------------------------------------
ALTER TABLE DEPT_EMP ADD CONSTRAINT DEP_DEPT_EMP_DEPT_NO_FK FOREIGN KEY(DEPT_NO)
        REFERENCES DEPARTMENTS(DEPT_NO) ENABLE;
ALTER TABLE DEPT_EMP ADD CONSTRAINT EMP_DEPT_EMP_EMP_NO_FK FOREIGN KEY(EMP_NO)
        REFERENCES EMPLOYEES(EMP_NO) ENABLE;

ALTER TABLE SALARIES ADD CONSTRAINT FK_SALARIES_EMPLOYEES FOREIGN KEY(EMP_NO)
      REFERENCES EMPLOYEES(EMP_NO) ENABLE;
----------------------------------------------------------------
-- Restrictii de tip cheie straina pentru tabela DEPT_MANAGER
----------------------------------------------------------------
ALTER TABLE DEPT_MANAGER ADD CONSTRAINT DEP_DEPT_MAN_DEPT_NO_FK FOREIGN KEY(DEPT_NO)
        REFERENCES DEPARTMENTS(DEPT_NO) ENABLE;
ALTER TABLE DEPT_MANAGER ADD CONSTRAINT EMP_DEST_MAN_EMP_NO_FK FOREIGN KEY(EMP_NO)
        REFERENCES EMPLOYEES(EMP_NO) ENABLE;
        
prompt #SCRIPT PROCESAT CU SUCCES
